windowsill-lab · phase 1

2026-07-23 · 2D Ising verification
Tonight I ran 2D Ising on an 128×128 lattice across 21 temperatures in [1.50, 3.50], 40,000 measurement sweeps each. The susceptibility peaked at T ≈ 2.300 ± 0.050; Onsager says T_c = 2.2692. Wall time on the GPU: 10.6s.
